SELECT [t].[ID], [t].[CropName], [t0].[ProductId], [t0].[ProductName], [t0].[CropId], [t0].[ID]
FROM (
    SELECT [c].[ID], [c].[CropName]
    FROM [CropMaster] AS [c]
    LEFT JOIN [ProductMaster] AS [p] ON [c].[ID] = [p].[CropId]
    GROUP BY [c].[ID], [c].[CropName]
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[ID] AS [ProductId], [p0].[ProductName], [p0].[CropId], [c0].[ID], [c0].[CropName]
    FROM [CropMaster] AS [c0]
    LEFT JOIN [ProductMaster] AS [p0] ON [c0].[ID] = [p0].[CropId]
    WHERE [p0].[ID] IS NOT NULL
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ID] = [t0].[ID] AND [t].[CropName] = [t0].[CropName]
ORDER BY [t].[ID], [t].[CropName], [t0].[ID]

SELECT @var0 = [d].[name]
FROM [sys].[default_constraints] [d]
INNER JOIN [sys].[columns] [c] ON [d].[parent_column_id] = [c].[column_id] AND [d].[parent_object_id] = [c].[object_id]
WHERE ([d].[parent_object_id] = OBJECT_ID(N'[CropMaster]') AND [c].[name] = N'Description');
